  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_9dee199d-4089-469a-8b65-be6d69be8de8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

Passion will ignite . . .<br /><br />Crystal Brook has always been the dud Savant in her family; paranormal powers just aren't her thing. Dropping out of school with a clutch of 'E' grades and no future, she lives in the shadow of her high-flying sister Diamond. On a trip to Denver, a chance encounter with the dashing Benedict brothers leaves Diamond head over heels in love and engaged to be married. Crystal, on the other hand, is unimpressed by their charms . . . in fact no boy can annoy her as much as Xav Benedict! Back in Venice, their families assemble for Diamond's wedding and a powerful enemy seizes the opportunity to attack. Crystal and Xav must join forces to save their loved-ones, unlocking a secret that, until now, has lain deeply buried . . .</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/246967778?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sam" href="/user/show/5933971-sam">Sam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer246967778" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15454578161954408314"><i>Seeking Crystal</i> is the third book in the intriguing and extremely gripping <i>Benedict</i> series. If your looking for a set of books to get obsessed over this year, make sure you pick up this series.<br/><br/>Crystal Brook doesn't seem to have paranormal powers like she should have been born with. She's not clever, she's not pretty and, to rub it all in her big nose, she's always been in the shadow of her successful older sister, Diamond. On a trip to Denver, a run-in with the gorgeous Benedict brothers leaves </span>
  <span id="freeText15454578161954408314" style="display:none"><i>Seeking Crystal</i> is the third book in the intriguing and extremely gripping <i>Benedict</i> series. If your looking for a set of books to get obsessed over this year, make sure you pick up this series.<br /><br />Crystal Brook doesn't seem to have paranormal powers like she should have been born with. She's not clever, she's not pretty and, to rub it all in her big nose, she's always been in the shadow of her successful older sister, Diamond. On a trip to Denver, a run-in with the gorgeous Benedict brothers leaves Diamond in love and engaged to be married with one of them. Crystal doesn't understand how everything could happen so fast, because unlike her sister she is unimpressed by the boys' charms. But could the most annoying of the boys, Xav, help her unlock a secret that could change Crystal's life?<br /><br />Stirling does an incredible job at keeping readers hooked and desperate to read more after just a few pages. Her characters are entertaining and very realistic. I've really enjoyed the characters from her previous books in the series and it was great to see that they played a part in this book. <br /><br />Moving away from the supporting characters, I was ecstatic to find out that this book was finally about Xav discovering his soulfinder. Those who have read the previous books will know that he is a sweet talker who cracks the best jokes. It was amazing to read about him and his blossoming relationship with Crystal; a very tall, dark-haired girl.<br /><br />This book is told from the POV of Crystal. Even though she is from a Savant family, she does not have the powers she should have been born with. She isn't clever and she isn't pretty, but she is strong-willed and determined. When she and Xav meet, boy, do sparks fly! Xav gets on her nerves like no other boy has before. Believe me, their encounter is hilarious. Scratch that, all scenes with Xav and Crystal in the same room are hilarious!<br /><br />Stirling does not disappoint fans with this extraordinary installment! The books just get better and better. New characters, more mysteries and lots more laughs to be had with the Benedict brothers. A fourth book? All I know is that it's going to be good.<br /><br />If you are interested in reading<i> Seeking Crystal </i>then I would recommend you read the first two books, <i>Finding Sky</i> and<i> Stealing Pheonix, </i>because it will give you a better idea of the characters and the world the books are set in.<br /><br /><a href="http://bookcrazedreviews.blogspot.com/2012/05/teaser-tuesday-2.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Guys, click here to read a teaser of Seeking Crystal!</a><br /><br /><a href="http://bookcrazedreviews.blogspot.com/2012/05/seeking-crystal-teasers.html&lt;br /&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">MORE TEASERS!</a></span>

<div id="review_330859402" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/330859402" />
    <a title="Serendipity Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1886570-serendipity-reviews"><img alt="Serendipity Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1392740916p2/1886570.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/330859402?book_show_action=true">May 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Serendipity Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Serendipity Reviews" href="/user/show/1886570-serendipity-reviews">Serendipity Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer330859402" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15577138299029861825">Oh now this is a really hard review to write. I really really loved the first two books in this series. I couldn't get enough of Finding Sky and Stealing Phoenix they were just so good, so it pains me to have to write anything negative at all about Seeking Crystal but I have to be honest and tell you how I felt.<br/>I didn't completely hate it, not by a long shot. I think the plot for this book was utterly AMAZING; I was absorbed in it from the very beginning. The secrets we discover about Crystal we</span>
  <span id="freeText15577138299029861825" style="display:none">Oh now this is a really hard review to write. I really really loved the first two books in this series. I couldn't get enough of Finding Sky and Stealing Phoenix they were just so good, so it pains me to have to write anything negative at all about Seeking Crystal but I have to be honest and tell you how I felt.<br />I didn't completely hate it, not by a long shot. I think the plot for this book was utterly AMAZING; I was absorbed in it from the very beginning. The secrets we discover about Crystal were pure genius. I can't wait to see what she does with her abilities in the future. I loved the fast paced feel of the book, as the drama unfolded and set of at break neck speed putting all of the Benedict brothers in danger. The inclusion of Steve, the hot American action man/superstar was a welcome addition to the story and I only hope the Brad Pitts and the Jason Stathams of the film world are as wonderful as he is. The setting of Venice was gorgeous and descriptive, allowing me to fall in love with a place I have yet to visit. <br />So you see I did enjoy the book, however I have a few gripes I feel I have to share. I can feel daggers being thrown at me by all the lovely loyal Benedict fans and I apologise in advance for my issues with this book.<br />Looking at it as a whole, I can see I have two overall problems with this book: timing and characterisation, which I have expanded on below. <br />Firstly with the timing, I struggled with the sudden development of the relationship between Trance and Diamond. I know that in these books 'instant love' is the norm;the Savants are supposed to find their soul finders and fall instantly in love, but I felt that it was a little bit rushed and extremely unbelievable, almost corny in parts. I found myself cringing as I read it. I felt that it had been written too quickly in order to get it out of the way, so the main story of Crystal and Xav could emerge. I would have loved to have seen it progress a little slower. With all the relationships so far in the book, they have taken a little time to progress, so I felt like I was being short changed a little. Also as soon as Xav and Crystal realised they had found their soul seeker, it was dealt with swiftly in order to get back to the plot. I wanted more. <br />As for characterisation, firstly, I didn't warm to Xav at all. In the previous two books I had liked him, but in this one he grated on my nerves. He wound me up by calling everyone 'darling' and 'cupcake'. I wasn't overly keen on Crystal either. I felt her change from the dud clumsy Savant to the wisest, most needed Savant a bit too fast a transformation. I was also surprised by her ability to make her own clothes within a few weeks of her new job with the designer. <br />I also had a problem with the characters I have loved from the previous two books. I wanted to see a progression within Sky and Phoenix, yet I felt nothing had really happened in their lives since we had last met them; they didn't really shine out in this book at all. I understand that this book isn't their story, but Crystals. However, it would have been lovely to see a bit of character development within their stories. <br />I apologise to all fans for being overly critical. Anyone who reads my blog regularly will know that isn't my style at all. I truly think it is because I have my editing head on at the moment, that I am picking up on things that wouldn't normally bother me. I think Joss Stirland is a talented author and I honestly loved the rest of the series, I just felt this book was the weakest from the three.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15577138299029861825" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText7459572095019081496" style="display:none">CAPTURING CAPTURING CAPTURING CAPTURING CAPTURING!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! Pleease let it be capturing instead of seeing. It sounds soooooooooooo much more romantic and exciting and dramatic!!!!!!!<br />Oh oh oh I can't wait for this book! I think I'm going to faint!<br />Uh what's that? It's going to be published in....2013?!............<br />*thud*<br /><br /><br />*****<br /><br />I don't know if I'm being too strict or too lenient. But I know one thing for sure - I am just too disappointed. I mean, when you've marked the release date of the book as on your birthday calendar, any outcome less than perfect will send you throwing yourself off the cliffs. You don't need a seer to tell you that. And even worse, for me, this book is slightly <i>less</i> than less than perfect.<br />Oh, don't mind me. I'm sure many readers would love this book. I hope they do. But something just went wrong for me. Yves and Phoenix set the bar too high. If I could transfer that book's ratings to this one, Seeking Crystal would receive 10 stars.<br />I'm not going to spoil this book for everyone. My opinion is strictly subjective. Joss Stirling's fan-base is more extensive and dangerous than what one can expect. Trust me, I was on the front line once, the moment I picked up Stealing Phoenix off the library bookshelves.<br />Half a year of waiting, intense speculation, faithful stalking, panic attacks, mood swings and depression has come down to this. Goodness knows what I'm supposed to be feeling right now.<br />Don't ask. Just. Don't.</span>

  <span id="freeText9102071489395264448" style="display:none">My favourite of the series yet! and Uriel and Victor better have different books... they define holy hotness!<br /><br />Sky's right at the end.. everyone has a soft spot for Xav.. including me! <br /><br /><b>"But thanks for worrying about me, Beauty."<br />"Please stop calling me that." I folded my arms across my chest.<br />"Fine." Drumming the steering wheel, he glanced at me briefly before turning back to the traffic. <br />"Hey, Beau—my respected and very equal cupcake, what’ve I done to annoy you? "<br /></b><br /><br />:O the blurb.. hehe love these types of stories.. just hope Diamond is not marrying the other Benedict brothers cos I want a different story for all of them! <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Trace doesn't get his story? -_- but, but... he's the other bad boyyyyyyyyyyy!!!!! and I was looking forward to his story :( <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_428981817" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/428981817" />
    <a title="Ferdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy"><img alt="Ferdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487898103p2/4596358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/428981817?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ferdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ferdy" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy">Ferdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer428981817" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1367881398534333544"><b>Spoilers</b><br/><br/>The third book in the series, the books revolve around the seven Benedict brothers, who are all Savants - people with special powers. Each brother is desperate to find their Soulfinders. Youngest brothers Zed and Yves found their heroines in the previous installments. This time around two of the Benedict brothers get their HEA.<br/>The story kicks off when oldest brother Trace finds his soulfinder in Diamond Brooke. Seconds after meeting they're kissing each other and planning their lives tog</span>
  <span id="freeText1367881398534333544" style="display:none"><b>Spoilers</b><br /><br />The third book in the series, the books revolve around the seven Benedict brothers, who are all Savants - people with special powers. Each brother is desperate to find their Soulfinders. Youngest brothers Zed and Yves found their heroines in the previous installments. This time around two of the Benedict brothers get their HEA.<br />The story kicks off when oldest brother Trace finds his soulfinder in Diamond Brooke. Seconds after meeting they're kissing each other and planning their lives together. Sadly and somewhat surprisingly, Trace and Diamond's meeting and eye roll inducing insta-love was the highlight of the book for me. The plot actually focuses on the boring romance between Diamond's younger sister, Crystal, and Trace's younger brother, Xavier. Why was the romance rubbish? Because I really really hated Crystal - she was a pig.<br />Crystal was a cookie cutter typical insecure, never been kissed, self pitying YA heroine. She kept moaning about how ugly she was but it turned out she was so pretty that she was offered top modeling jobs, she was bitter because she had rubbish powers but naturally she found out her powers were actually awesome, she thought she wasn't a speshul snowflake but surprise, surprise, she's actually the most speshulest snowflake of all the speshul snowflakes. She was so full of irritating cliches..ugh.<br />Xavier I guess was a decent enough love interest, unfortunately his love for Crystal just annoyed the hell out of me. I honestly don't know what he saw in <i>whingy-moany-mummy-doesn't-love-me</i> Crystal.<br />The plot was boring, the romance got on my nerves because the heroine was a pathetic bitch, most of the characters were cheesy and on top of all that there was a whole preachy vibe going on about forgiveness and shit...ugh.<br />On another note, I'm finding it annoying how the lives of the heroes in the series never change when they meet the heroine — their home life, dreams and plans stay the same yet the heroine always has to move or change any plans she once had just to be with the hero...ugh.<br />The first two books were pretty good — the main characters were likeable enough so I could forgive them being just the same old standard, run of the mill paranormal YA. This however was utterly disappointing as the main character was too much of a silly cow for me to enjoy it. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1367881398534333544" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_305857177" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/305857177" />
    <a title="Rimsa Ivashkov " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4386549-rimsa-ivashkov"><img alt="Rimsa Ivashkov " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1405092937p2/4386549.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/305857177?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rimsa Ivashkov " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rimsa Ivashkov " href="/user/show/4386549-rimsa-ivashkov">Rimsa Ivashkov </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer305857177" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5713619201106097981"><b>‘Another piggyback?’<br/>‘No, my pride can’t take it.’ He sat down on the hump of the bridge and pulled off his Timberlands. He thrust them in my arms. ‘Here, hold these. Don’t, whatever you do, drop them.’ Then before I could think what he intended, he swept me into his arms and strode into the calf-deep water.<br/>‘Xav! I’ve boots on—there’s no need.’<br/>He hugged me closer. ‘There’s every need, my lady. Have you not read the Gentleman’s Guide to Gallantry?’<br/>I shook my head, giggling as he hissed when his to</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5713619201106097981" style="display:none"><b>‘Another piggyback?’<br />‘No, my pride can’t take it.’ He sat down on the hump of the bridge and pulled off his Timberlands. He thrust them in my arms. ‘Here, hold these. Don’t, whatever you do, drop them.’ Then before I could think what he intended, he swept me into his arms and strode into the calf-deep water.<br />‘Xav! I’ve boots on—there’s no need.’<br />He hugged me closer. ‘There’s every need, my lady. Have you not read the Gentleman’s Guide to Gallantry?’<br />I shook my head, giggling as he hissed when his toes registered the cold water.<br />‘On page twenty-eight, it definitely says something about being drummed out of the ranks if a gentleman accepts a second piggyback from a lady. He must sacrifice his toes to keep her dry.’</b><br /><br />I absolutely loved this series, so I was beyond excited to read Seeking Crystal. Needless to say, I was expecting to be blown away by it, and thats exactly what happened. The book is just a pure joy to read with zero moements of boredom. The story never drags and it pulls you in so completely that you wouldnt be able to stop reading until you'd finished it. I love Joss Stirling's writing style, it so easy to get into and it flows perfectly. <br /><br />The best thing about this book is definitely the characters. I loved the Benedicts from the previous books, and they were just as hot as before. Xavier is my favourite though, so it was awesome to read a book with him as the hero. Xav is so sweet and full of charm and is always cracking a joke and making people swoon, but he's also very protective and compassionate and I absolutely adored him. Crystal was a brilliant new character and my favourite protagonist of the series. She thinks she's ugly and feels like she's the family screw up because she doesnt have any special savant abilities, but there's so much more to her than that. She's a really likeable character and very relatable. She's also pretty witty herself and can keep up with Xav's teasing. Thats why they were such a perfect match. They have earned a place in my top 5 YA couples and Xav's in my top YA crushes &lt;3 Their relationship was very cute and I enjoyed the build up and the sexual tension a lot. Their scenes together were swoon-worthy and perfect and I just couldnt get enough of them. <br /><br />You still meet old characters and it was great to see them again and how their relationships are now. The plot was great, with twists I hadnt predicted and so much new info was revealed, which I freakin loved. I'm not sure if its the last book or not, but I really hope not. From what we find out in this book, there is so much more that could happen. Victor's story could be very interesting from what we learn, especially because he's so mysterious and I would love to learn more about him and read his story. I'll keep my fingers crossed that there are more, because I'm addicted to this series. I recommend this to EVERYONE!!!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5713619201106097981" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_323650102" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/323650102" />
    <a title="Emma " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3342102-emma"><img alt="Emma " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586199150p2/3342102.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/323650102?book_show_action=true">May 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emma " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emma " href="/user/show/3342102-emma">Emma </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer323650102" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer710376999724266656">Best one yet - love it<br/><br/>Please bear in mind that this is the third book in the series and the review may contain spoilers for the previous books.<br/><br/>I adore this series so so so much, I was querying whether this was the last book in the series earlier today and Joss very kindly posted THIS on her blog. So fingers crossed we will be seeing more of the Benedicts in the future.<br/><br/>Seeking Crystal manages to tie together outstanding elements of the plot from the previous 2 books. It never ceases to amaze me h</span>
  <span id="freeText710376999724266656" style="display:none">Best one yet - love it<br /><br />Please bear in mind that this is the third book in the series and the review may contain spoilers for the previous books.<br /><br />I adore this series so so so much, I was querying whether this was the last book in the series earlier today and Joss very kindly posted THIS on her blog. So fingers crossed we will be seeing more of the Benedicts in the future.<br /><br />Seeking Crystal manages to tie together outstanding elements of the plot from the previous 2 books. It never ceases to amaze me how the title of the books in this series offers hints as to the plot. It is just brilliant.<br /><br />Crystal is a very different character to those we have previously encountered in the previous books. Utterly out of place in a family of savants due to her lack of paranormal powers. I really felt for Crystal; she’s not especially close to her mother who favors the savants of the family. She is, however, very close to her father, who is able to see just how special Crystal is with or without paranormal powers. His death is a devastating blow to the family but even more so for Crystal who felt he was the only person to understand her.<br /><br />The relationship between soul-finders is examined closely and at a far deeper level than the previous books bringing a greater level of understanding to the story as a whole. With the death of Crystal’s father it allows insight into how it feels to lose your soul-finder and also examines savants decisions to either wait and hope for their soul-finder or chance happiness with someone you know isn’t you’re other half. The depiction of heartbreak and being set adrift translates as an integral part of the plot in more ways than one.<br /><br />The setting is quite simply beautiful,the richly descriptive, sensory writing not only aids the imagery but actually transports you into the story. The changing locations for this series alongside the introduction of new characters ensures that the plot remains fresh. Although I will say again that I am always amazed how Joss Stirling manages to create a whole new story while tying the previous plot thread and characters into it. All of the previous characters are included, it takes a very skillful writer to develop this amount of characters and their relationships simultaneously.<br /><br />There are some amazing revelations that I will honestly say I did not see coming but I am not going to spoil the story for you by telling you about them.<br /><br />This series just goes from strength to strength, I for one am certainly not ready to say goodbye quite yet. Let’s hope there is more of the Benedicts to come.</span>
  <a data-text-id="710376999724266656" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/860963253" />
    <a title="Steffi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4676630-steffi"><img alt="Steffi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594970123p2/4676630.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/860963253?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6669598499730396149">Seeking Crystal has been my favourite story from the Savant world.<br/>The story was kind of grabbing me and I really liked Crystal and her sister. <br/><br/>This book had the same flaws as the other 2 books of the trilogy. There is no chemistry and the soulfinder thing just doesn't feel like as special as it is supposed to be. The problems are solved way too easily.<br/><br/>I will finish this series at this point and will probably won't read any further books in this series.</span>

<div id="review_351954882" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/351954882" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/351954882?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-print">books-i-own-print</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=british-author">british-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=for-review-read">for-review-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=amazon-vine">amazon-vine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer351954882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13336391437151898132">Crystal comes from a large family of Savants but she has always felt like a failure compared to her brothers and sisters, she is the only one who isn't able to communicate telepathically and she has the most useless Savant ability ever. The only thing she is any good at is finding things that people have lost - so she's the person who her family turn to when they lose their car keys but not for much else. Crystal has travelled to Denver with her sister Diamond for a conference arranged by the Be</span>
  <span id="freeText13336391437151898132" style="display:none">Crystal comes from a large family of Savants but she has always felt like a failure compared to her brothers and sisters, she is the only one who isn't able to communicate telepathically and she has the most useless Savant ability ever. The only thing she is any good at is finding things that people have lost - so she's the person who her family turn to when they lose their car keys but not for much else. Crystal has travelled to Denver with her sister Diamond for a conference arranged by the Benedicts and it is there that Diamond immediately recognises Trace as her Soulfinder and the couple are quickly engaged to be married. Back at their home in Venice Crystal is in charge of organising Diamond's hen party and she is in competition with Trace's brother Xav for who can come up with the best night out. Xav and Crystal have taken an instant dislike for each other but when the family come under attack and several of the Soulfinders are taken hostage it is up to the two of them to figure out how to save the others.<br /><br />I'm a massive fan of this series so have been looking forward to reading Seeking Crystal for ages now and I'm pleased to say that it was everything I hoped it would be. Fans of the series are sure to enjoy this instalment just as much as the previous ones and I'm really hoping that this isn't the last we have seen of the Benedicts - please someone tell me there will be another book! The romance between Diamond and Trace does move incredibly quickly but as they aren't the main characters for this book I felt that was understandable. Especially when you consider that they are both much older than Crystal and Xav so have been waiting a long time for their Soulfinder to come along, knowing full well that they might never find them. It made sense to me that they would accept their relationship much faster, they are both confident in who and what they are and are delighted to find the missing piece of themselves.<br /><br />Crystal wasn't always the easiest character to like, at times she could be very childish and I got frustrated with her and the temper tantrums she threw but at the same time I could understand why she was so upset. She has spent her whole life feeling like she is useless and when she finally finds something that she thinks she could be good at her family are completely against the idea. I did feel that Diamond and Trace could have done a much better job of explaining to her why modelling wasn't such a great idea but she worked it out for herself eventually. When things start to go wrong and Diamond and other family members disappear Crystal really does step up to the plate and show how strong she can be. I loved the developments with her abilities and think that will add a really interesting element to any future books we might see.<br /><br />I really liked Xav, he could be cocky and arrogant but he often tended to put on an act and deep down he was a really nice guy. He knew how to push Crystal's buttons and went out of his way to irritate her but that was just his way of teasing the newest member of his family. It was obvious from the beginning that they were attracted to each other but not believing they were Soulfinders meant there was no point in pursuing things further. Xav's power as a healer makes him very protective of everyone around him, he wants to be able to keep everyone safe and finds it distressing that he was unable to stop his family members being hurt. I really loved the banter between Xav and Crystal, the way they constantly snipped at each other was fun to watch but they grew to respect each other when they started working together.<br /><br />I loved the Venice setting for this story, the previous books were set in Denver and London so it was nice to visit somewhere different. I've never been to Venice (it's somewhere I always wanted to go) but the descriptions were so well done that it really felt like I was there and I was able to picture things very clearly. I have to say that the plot of Seeking Crystal was the best of the series so far, the story was fast paced, action packed and included some great new side characters. We also got to see some of the previous characters which was nice although the circumstances didn't allow us to catch up with the girls as much as I would have liked. I loved getting to see the Benedict boys all working so well together though, they certainly prove themselves a force to be reckoned with! I'd definitely recommend this series to fans of YA paranormal romance, I think you could probably get away with reading this as a standalone novel but personally I think the series works much better if you read them in order. If you've not already read Finding Sky and Stealing Phoenix then you really don't know what you're missing.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13336391437151898132" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10731552601962655878">This review was originally published at <a href='http://www.flutteringbutterflies.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fluttering Butterflies</a><br/><br/>Oh lordy, do I absolutely LOVE the Benedict brothers. Really and truly, I love them. And I loved this latest installment, which pairs up two of the Benedict brothers with sisters Diamond and Crystal.<br/><br/>I really felt for Crystal, the main character of this story. She's always been treated a bit badly by her family for being a dud savant. She has no powers, she's not great with schooling. She really figures herself to have no real future, </span>
  <span id="freeText10731552601962655878" style="display:none">This review was originally published at <a href="http://www.flutteringbutterflies.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Fluttering Butterflies</a><br /><br />Oh lordy, do I absolutely LOVE the Benedict brothers. Really and truly, I love them. And I loved this latest installment, which pairs up two of the Benedict brothers with sisters Diamond and Crystal.<br /><br />I really felt for Crystal, the main character of this story. She's always been treated a bit badly by her family for being a dud savant. She has no powers, she's not great with schooling. She really figures herself to have no real future, and that of course, is a feeling that is one that many including myself has felt before. But things begin to change for Crystal, when her older sister, Diamond meets her soul-finder amongst the famous Benedict family of crime-fighters. While happy for her sister, Crystal finds herself hugely annoyed by Diamond's new family, especially Xav. But in the process of planning Diamond's wedding, things go very, very wrong and Crystal and Xav will have to get over their issues to help each other out. <br /><br />I really loved the setting of Venice. It just seems a very romantic and magical place to fight against evil and to fall in love. I also loved the transformation of Crystal from kicked-puppy at the beginning of the book to getting used to the very different turns her life has taken. It was fun to see some familiar faces from the previous books and also to witness some different abilities and means of attack. <br /><br />I really hope this series continues! I know all we have left are some of the older brothers which could possibly stray out of the YA market, but I still want to know what will happen, especially after the brief sneak peek we get at the end of this book!</span>

<div id="review_1645751650" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1645751650" />
    <a title="Zina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13999485-zina"><img alt="Zina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1495649372p2/13999485.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1645751650?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zina" href="/user/show/13999485-zina">Zina</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer4527225306369039182">The first half of this was soo slow and I found some of the 'romance' aspects very cringey. The second half was better. FULL REVIEW TO COME<br/><br/><i>

  <span id="freeText4527225306369039182" style="display:none">The first half of this was soo slow and I found some of the 'romance' aspects very cringey. The second half was better. FULL REVIEW TO COME<br><br><i>
  <b>“Xavier, you have given me more grey hairs than all my sons put together.’ Saul frowned, then corrected himself. ‘To be fair, you and Zed. Just try not to add to them tonight.”</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://www.paein-and-ms4tune.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394986555i/8932321._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br><b>My review can also be found <a href="http://www.paein-and-ms4tune.co.uk/?p=3740" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></b><br><br>I just love this series. I love Joss Stirling’s portrayal of family love and endurance. It doesn’t matter what life throws at the Benedict family, they are convinced that love can concur all, and in this book you really need to hold onto that belief as Joss Stirling, throws in a doozy of a storyline that leave the Benedict men with a possible future without their Soulfinders!<br><br>Two Benedict brothers find their Soulfinders in this book, Trace and (my favourite brother) Xav.<br><br>The main character is Crystal the youngest daughter of a large Savant family. While all her brothers and sisters have an amazing Savant gift – such as Diamond who can influence peoples emotions, so works as a peacemaker – Crystal doesn’t seem to have a gift, well she does but her’s seems pointless in comparison. She can find things, you know like lost keys etc. But Crystal feels she’s a dud within her Savant family as she is unable to use telepathy, the main benefit of being a Savant. If she tries. She throws up. And if she can’t use telepathy how will she ever know her Soulfinder?<br><br>The only complaint I have about this new installment was the childish approach to Diamond (Crystal’s big sister) and Trace’s relationship. It was very one dimensional and unrealistic and as a result actually made me cringe in places! It just lacked the depth that I would have expected. They met, they fell instantly in love, and started planning their wedding! Wow, come on…. seriously? And annoyingly this seemed to be the focal point of the first half of the book. We watch all this from Crystal point of view. Which is the only thing that made it bearable, but also may explain the flatness that I experienced. I wish we’d got onto Crystal and Xav’s storyline quicker because that was adorable. Again there were a few moments where I wish there had been a bit more explanation. Such as when Crystal finally unlocked her ‘Skill’. (I’m still no clear on how this happened) as this was the moment that Xav and Crystal finally discover their bond and as I was so confused I felt I didn’t really get the whole Awwwww factor!<br><br>As usual there is a bad guy to defeat and a mystery to solve and this was amazing. I love it when all the Benedict’s band together to fight crime. They always have each others backs.<br><br>Overall a little childish in places but it’s a good read either way. And, if you love the Benedict’s as much as I do, then you won’t be disappointed.</span>

<div id="review_386833622" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/386833622" />
    <a title="Lyndsey O&#39;Halloran" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3850088-lyndsey-o-halloran"><img alt="Lyndsey O&#39;Halloran" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1276289261p2/3850088.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/386833622?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lyndsey O&#39;Halloran" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lyndsey O&#39;Halloran" href="/user/show/3850088-lyndsey-o-halloran">Lyndsey O&#39;Halloran</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3850088-lyndsey-o-halloran?shelf=ya">ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer386833622" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7020851137374154073">The setting for this book is very different from the others in the series. Crystal and her sister Diamond head to Denver for a very quick trip but there, Diamond manages to meet her Soulfinder. This is a massive deal for all Savants, which Crystal and Diamond both are and it sets the scene for the rest of the book. Although this book is about Crystal, Diamond finding her other half means heading back to Venice, where they live so that a wedding can be planned. I really liked that Denver was incl</span>
  <span id="freeText7020851137374154073" style="display:none">The setting for this book is very different from the others in the series. Crystal and her sister Diamond head to Denver for a very quick trip but there, Diamond manages to meet her Soulfinder. This is a massive deal for all Savants, which Crystal and Diamond both are and it sets the scene for the rest of the book. Although this book is about Crystal, Diamond finding her other half means heading back to Venice, where they live so that a wedding can be planned. I really liked that Denver was included, if only for a little bit, as the setting had been such a big part of the other books. However, I loved that Stirling took the characters to Venice too because it was magical. <br /><br />I really liked Crystal as a main character. She comes from a large family, is the seventh child and thinks that her Savant abilities are faulty. She cannot do telepathy with anyone as it makes her physically sick and her actual ability is to find things… like lost keys. Not quite as impressive as being able to make fire with your hands or being able to heal someone is it? Crystal had a great voice and even though she was down some of the time, she was still quite outspoken and funny. I really liked her narrative voice and it made reading the book exciting and very entertaining. <br /><br />I know some people have said that they didn’t like Xav too much in this book but I loved him. He is a great match for Crystal as he is just as outspoken and funny. He stands out in comparison to his brothers due to his charm (in its own strange way) and the way he speaks to people, especially Crystal. He has great nicknames for her such as Cupcake, which she hated which made it even funnier. I really enjoyed reading about Xav and watching his relationship with Crystal develop. <br /><br />Crystal and Xav’s relationship is different from the others in this series due to it not being love at first sight. To begin with, Crystal cannot stand the sight of Xav and when they are forced together because of the wedding, Crystal cannot think of anything worse than being stuck with him. The banter between the two characters was part of what made them both so likeable. Each gave as good as it gets and it was great to see them both getting annoyed with each other. <br /><br />The plot was also one of the best in the series so far for me too. Stirling brings together new plot aspects mixed in with things that happened in previous books which was a good way to tie everything together. There are quite a lot of shocking things which happen in this book and I wasn’t expecting a lot of them. Crystal’s Savant ability takes up a large part of this book but it was woven in with everything else, taking some of the attention off of her and bringing in all of the other characters. If you thought Stealing Phoenix was exciting then you will be blown away by Seeking Crystal. This book has the excitement of an action film and things happening all over the place. <br /><br />Seeking Crystal is by far my favourite in this series so far because it had everything I could possibly want! Joss Stirling can do no wrong in my eyes! </span>
  <a data-text-id="7020851137374154073" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_298117108" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/298117108" />
    <a title="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life"><img alt="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563622982p2/3024878.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/298117108?book_show_action=true">Mar 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" href="/user/show/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life">Donna {Book Passion For Life}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=ya-paranormal-romance">ya-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer298117108" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10399917006531123888"><i>Seeking Crystal</i> is book three in the Benedict series and author Joss Stirling is still going strong. This is one of my favourite series - ever, and they just get better and better with each book. <br/><br/>This time around we see Crystal Brooks - who has always been apart of the Savant world, however she feels more disconnected then everyone towards her gift. It hardly works and it makes her feel sick. So when her sister, Diamond finds her soul finder in Tracy Benedict, Crystal has no choice but to meet t</span>
  <span id="freeText10399917006531123888" style="display:none"><i>Seeking Crystal</i> is book three in the Benedict series and author Joss Stirling is still going strong. This is one of my favourite series - ever, and they just get better and better with each book. <br /><br />This time around we see Crystal Brooks - who has always been apart of the Savant world, however she feels more disconnected then everyone towards her gift. It hardly works and it makes her feel sick. So when her sister, Diamond finds her soul finder in Tracy Benedict, Crystal has no choice but to meet the rest of his family, including Xav Benedict who as you can guess, becomes her soul finder but there are some unexpected twists along the way. While planning for Diamond's wedding the Brooks and Benedicts come together but it's not long before trouble coming looking for the Benedicts and now, Crystal and Xav must join together to saved their families. <br /><br />I loved it, just loved it! I don't think I could ever be disappointed with Joss Stirling's work because there's so much love and magic that goes into her stories, which makes them become beautiful reads, and Seeking Crystal is nothing short of amazing. What I enjoyed about this story so much was not only did we get to see one brother find his soul finder but we found two. So this time around, we get two for the price of one. <br /><br />I've always been a massive fan of Xav's so, I was thrilled this book was about him. I adore his personality, he's very funny and he does love himself just a little bit but he's admiral, caring and honest. We've always seen him as the player out of the all the other brothers, so it was great to see him find the one for him. Now Crystal, I liked her, I really did but she was very stubborn. Not that that made me dislike her in any way but because she's stubborn, she makes rash decisions that cloud her mind. I love her and Xav's relationship because it was so different from the other brothers. I won't tell you any more because I don't want to spoil it for you but be prepared to be shocked. And Crystal comes with many secrets...especially one secret that she doesn't even know herself and let me tell you, what a game changer it is. I can not wait to see where Joss takes this, it really was a mind-blowing game changer. <br /><br /><i>Seeking Crystal</i> is definitely one of my favourites out of the series. It's adventuress, engaging and very captivating - one full of hope, love and hidden secrets and I loved every single minute of it. I can not wait for book four in the series and I'm dying to find out who it will feature this time. <br /><br /><b>A big thank you to Oxford University Publishing for giving me the opportunity to review this book. </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10399917006531123888" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_579882933" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/579882933" />
    <a title="Rebecca" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7377944-rebecca"><img alt="Rebecca" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1373472189p2/7377944.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/579882933?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rebecca" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rebecca" href="/user/show/7377944-rebecca">Rebecca</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer579882933" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8060654491402484339">At the beginning of the book, we are introduced to two of the main characters, sisters Crystal and Diamond, who are away on a business trip. At the very beginning of the book Diamond finds her soulmate, Trace, or her 'soulfinder' as they are known in this series. The two sisters meet the rest of Trace's family, and Crystal develops an instant dislike to Xav, one of the other Benedict brothers. <br/>Crystal, unlike other savants, doesn't have an 'amazing' talent, as she sees it, she is actually quite </span>
  <span id="freeText8060654491402484339" style="display:none">At the beginning of the book, we are introduced to two of the main characters, sisters Crystal and Diamond, who are away on a business trip. At the very beginning of the book Diamond finds her soulmate, Trace, or her 'soulfinder' as they are known in this series. The two sisters meet the rest of Trace's family, and Crystal develops an instant dislike to Xav, one of the other Benedict brothers. <br />Crystal, unlike other savants, doesn't have an 'amazing' talent, as she sees it, she is actually quite ordinary. She's also tall and lanky, with an unusual look about her. One thing I dislike about this book is how much Crystal herself goes on about this, constantly feeling sorry for herself. I also dislike how much she pushes Xav away to begin with. <br />Diamond and Trace want to be married as soon as possible, and through this and her general actions, we see how patronising she can be towards Crystal. Hm. I don't know if it's just me, or the length of time I waited before reading the second two books, but I'm not liking them as much as I did Finding Sky. <br />Crystal has gone back to her home in Rome and gotten herself a job as a costume maker- one thing in the book which does appeal to me; designing and making traditional Venetian costume masks etc, which adds to the fantasy feel of the book.<br /><br />Now we're beginning to see Xav and Crystal's relationship develop, and the storyline is getting a bit more interesting. Towards the second half of the book, the story really picks up and you really don't know which way it's going to go, so it keeps you wanting to read on. <br />A good sequel to the other Benedict books. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8060654491402484339" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6848046563927400012">It started really boring but I liked it in the end. <br/><br/>We have a tall female protagonist! Practically unseen! <br/><br/>What I liked about this book was her ability! So different and unique! Finally the Benedicts brothers can find their soulmates! ALL OF THEM. <br/><br/>So, the book started with Crystal and her sister Diamond being attacked by muggers, and who finds them? Obviously a Benedict. Trace and Diamond become Soulfinders, and kiss and kiss, while Crystal, injured on the floor waited patienly for them to stop.</span>
  <span id="freeText6848046563927400012" style="display:none">It started really boring but I liked it in the end. <br /><br />We have a tall female protagonist! Practically unseen! <br /><br />What I liked about this book was her ability! So different and unique! Finally the Benedicts brothers can find their soulmates! ALL OF THEM. <br /><br />So, the book started with Crystal and her sister Diamond being attacked by muggers, and who finds them? Obviously a Benedict. Trace and Diamond become Soulfinders, and kiss and kiss, while Crystal, injured on the floor waited patienly for them to stop. I would have shouted something at them. <br /><br />Then she met Xav and sparks flew. It isn't until the other women soulfinders are kidnapped that he learned about her ability and her bond to Xav. <br /><br />The girls had their soulfinders totally whipped from their minds. That was really sad, seeing the guys suffering so much. But I love the kick ass team that are the Benedicts. LOVE THEM! <br /><br />I laughed so hard with Steve, and his hero aspiration. He was awesome! At first he was kind of annoyed and self- centered but I loved him at the end. Glad that Crystal found out that Lily was the love of her life. <br /><br />I'm so happy for this ending: Xav and Crystal together, Zed and Sky, Phee and Yves married and Diamond and Trace getting to. Love this trilogy! Unfortunately, there's no more books. I'm gonna miss the Benedicts brothers! <br /><br />My favourite was : <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10410278.Stealing_Phoenix__Benedicts___2_" title="Stealing Phoenix (Benedicts, #2) by Joss Stirling" rel="nofollow noopener">Stealing Phoenix</a>, then <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8314214.Finding_Sky__Benedicts___1_" title="Finding Sky (Benedicts, #1) by Joss Stirling" rel="nofollow noopener">Finding Sky</a> , and then this one, but you can't help loving all the brothers!</span>

<div id="review_307830235" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/307830235" />
    <a title="Jasz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8632318-jasz"><img alt="Jasz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379189937p2/8632318.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/307830235?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasz" href="/user/show/8632318-jasz">Jasz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">everyone who can enjoy a good book</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8632318-jasz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8632318-jasz?shelf=finished-series">finished-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer307830235" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16420611016586676649">Do you know what it's like to laugh that much, your cheeks hurt? Well I do, Xav is just so funny!<br/><br/>This book is certainly worth of 5 stars, nothing less. I really enjoyed this book, it's exciting and I could't put it away. I really don't know how Joss does it, most of the time when I read the sequel of a book, I expect the first one to be the best. But every book is just as good as the last one, if not, even better.<br/><br/>The quote I loved the most and that stayed with me was: "Sometimes the comedy stops</span>
  <span id="freeText16420611016586676649" style="display:none">Do you know what it's like to laugh that much, your cheeks hurt? Well I do, Xav is just so funny!<br /><br />This book is certainly worth of 5 stars, nothing less. I really enjoyed this book, it's exciting and I could't put it away. I really don't know how Joss does it, most of the time when I read the sequel of a book, I expect the first one to be the best. But every book is just as good as the last one, if not, even better.<br /><br />The quote I loved the most and that stayed with me was: "Sometimes the comedy stops people realizing you can be hurt as much as someone of a more serious character". <br />And yes people, you probably already guessed it but: THAT'S ME. I totally recognize myself in that sentence. This quote is so true. When you laugh the whole time, people are shocked to see just a single tear escaping your eyes.<br /><br />Another good thing about this book: it wasn't hard to understand, you didn't have to think, just 'go with the flow'.<br /><br />I really hope there's a forth book on the way. I simply can't get enough of the characters. I really hope people can agree with me ... =D<br /><br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer940195736824941325">Xav<br/>Crystal <br/><br/><i>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br/>Blurb: Sparks will fly . . . Passion will ignite . . .<br/><br/>Crystal Brook has always been the dud Savant in her family; paranormal powers just aren't her thing. Dropping out of school with a clutch of 'E' grades and no future, she lives in the shadow of her high-flying sister Diamond. On a trip to Denver, a chance encounter with the dashing Benedict brothers leaves Diamond head over heels in love and engaged to be married. Crystal, on the other hand, is unimpressed by th</i></span>
  <span id="freeText940195736824941325" style="display:none">Xav<br />Crystal <br /><br /><i>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br />Blurb: Sparks will fly . . . Dropping out of school with a clutch of 'E' grades and no future, she lives in the shadow of her high-flying sister Diamond. On a trip to Denver, a chance encounter with the dashing Benedict brothers leaves Diamond head over heels in love and engaged to be married. Crystal, on the other hand, is unimpressed by their charms . . . in fact no boy can annoy her as much as Xav Benedict! Back in Venice, their families assemble for Diamond's wedding and a powerful enemy seizes the opportunity to attack. Crystal and Xav must join forces to save their loved-ones, unlocking a secret that, until now, has lain deeply buried . . . <br />~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~</i></span>

  <span id="freeText1610204692493917898" style="display:none">Joss continues the line of good books, and i love the new setting of Venice. Even though i think that finding sky will always be my favorite of the novels, i did like this new novel better than her second, but that may just be personal preferance to the brothers. It had a gripping ending and left the stories future wide open. The characters were lovable and i always seemed to put Xaiv and Crystal against the world. It was also quite intresting to have a fully functional european savent family and to see how their family ties compared to the Benedicts. I also liked the fact that Crystals past was not too dramatic, otherwise it may have seemed like it was simply tying to outdo Sky and Phoenix. But overall beautiful setting, and intresting storyline, if there is another Benedict book on the way i think i will be continuing.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9iT4HVA2StZ59lt+W8kk8XATmvwkZCrSQuVwZW1GeRAJuVv/Q2RS5iLKvrJXE7mrE4TmOWRqQPjEkP7LtMKtuw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zMGPP7MqbaaIp2ntcJwMgoSkSZymRqIJJFRrQOiZAhUzXCzdoHh1ltObjCF8RpHY5zM1WeZIyCOiIeXuMR3Wvg==')})
  }

Арогантен, дистанциран и избухлив, той е взел страха на всички от гимназията в Уикенридж - съученици и учители. Дори на новото момиче Скай, която не желае да признае пред себе си, че изпитва и силно привличане към възмутително добре изглеждащия Зед. И тогава внезапно тя чува неговия глас в ума си... той чете нейните мисли и говори в съзнанието й. А Зед разбира, че Скай е сродната му душа, идеалната му половина и савант като него самия. Скай не вярва на думите му, че е човек със свръхестествени сили. <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer8454090490250964656">Joss Stirling is a British novelist. Her first novel under this name was the internationally successful, Finding Sky, which is followed by five others in the same series entering into the savant world of young people with special powers. Central to the story are the Benedict Brothers, seven talented guys from Colorado. <br/><br/>In a second series, Struck, Joss begins a new world of detective romance. The f</span>
  <span id="freeText8454090490250964656" style="display:none">Joss Stirling is a British novelist. Her first novel under this name was the internationally successful, Finding Sky, which is followed by five others in the same series entering into the savant world of young people with special powers. Central to the story are the Benedict Brothers, seven talented guys from Colorado. <br /><br />In a second series, Struck, Joss begins a new world of detective romance. The first three parts are: Struck (#1) and Stung (#2), and Shaken (#3) and Scorched (#4). Joss introduces readers to four new heroes - Kieran Storm, Nathan Hunter, Joe Masters and Damien Castle, who all attention the Young Detective Agency. The first part, Struck, won the Romantic Novel of the Year 2015 in the UK.<br /><br />Her new series, PERIL, a paranormal love story set in the near future, is out 13 July 2017.<br /><br />Joss lives in Oxford, England. She is married with three children.<br /><br /><br />Stirling also publishes under two pen names: Julia Golding and Eve Edwards.</span>
